I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
MERGE should raise when multiple source rows match target row
# Environment

**Delta-rs version**: 0.16.4

**Binding**: Python 0.16.4

**Environment**:
- **Cloud provider**: None
- **OS**: MacOS Sonoma 14.4
- **Other**:

***
# Bug

**What happened**:
TableMerger.when_matched_update_all() inserts records when there is a match on multiple source columns
TableMerger.when_matched_update() inserts records when there is a match on multiple source columns


**What you expected to happen**:
TableMerger.when_matched_update_all() should throw an error if a target record matches multiple source records 
TableMerger.when_matched_update() should throw an error if a target record matches multiple source records 

They should never insert new records.

**How to reproduce it**:
Using polars 0.20.7
```python
import polars as pl
from deltalake import DeltaTable

base_df = pl.DataFrame(
    {
        "id": [1, 2],
        "attr": ["x", "y"]
    }
)

base_df.write_delta("./test_cdc", mode="overwrite")

dt = DeltaTable("./test_cdc")

print(pl.DataFrame(dt.to_pyarrow_table()))

cdc_df = pl.DataFrame(
    {
        "id": [1,1,1,2,2],
        "attr": ["a","b","c","d","e"],
        "op": ["U", "U", "U", "U", "U"]
    }
)


(
    dt.merge(
        cdc_df.to_arrow(),
        "s.id = t.id",
        source_alias="s",
        target_alias="t",
    )
    .when_matched_update(
        updates={"t.attr": "s.attr"},
        predicate="s.op = 'U'")
    .execute()
)

print(pl.DataFrame(dt.to_pyarrow_table()))
```

Gives the following output

**base table**
```bash
shape: (2, 2)
┌─────┬──────┐
│ id  ┆ attr │
│ --- ┆ ---  │
│ i64 ┆ str  │
╞═════╪══════╡
│ 1   ┆ x    │
│ 2   ┆ y    │
└─────┴──────┘
```

**After TableMerger is executed**
```bash
shape: (5, 2)
┌─────┬──────┐
│ id  ┆ attr │
│ --- ┆ ---  │
│ i64 ┆ str  │
╞═════╪══════╡
│ 2   ┆ d    │
│ 2   ┆ e    │
│ 1   ┆ a    │
│ 1   ┆ b    │
│ 1   ┆ c    │
└─────┴──────┘
```
**More details**:
Info on the specific case in slack: https://delta-users.slack.com/archives/C013LCAEB98/p1712673309723829

     1	//! Merge data from a source dataset with the target Delta Table based on a join
     2	//! predicate.  A full outer join is performed which results in source and
     3	//! target records that match, source records that do not match, or target
     4	//! records that do not match.
     5	//!
     6	//! Users can specify update, delete, and insert operations for these categories
     7	//! and specify additional predicates for finer control. The order of operations
     8	//! specified matter.  See [`MergeBuilder`] for more information
     9	//!
    10	//! # Example
    11	//! ```rust ignore
    12	//! let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;
    13	//! let (table, metrics) = DeltaOps(table)
    14	//!     .merge(source, col("target.id").eq(col("source.id")))
    15	//!     .with_source_alias("source")
    16	//!     .with_target_alias("target")
    17	//!     .when_matched_update(|update| {
    18	//!         update
    19	//!             .update("value", col("source.value") + lit(1))
    20	//!             .update("modified", col("source.modified"))
    21	//!     })?
    22	//!     .when_not_matched_insert(|insert| {
    23	//!         insert
    24	//!             .set("id", col("source.id"))
    25	//!             .set("value", col("source.value"))
    26	//!             .set("modified", col("source.modified"))
    27	//!     })?
    28	//!     .await?
    29	//! ````

   132	/// Merge records into a Delta Table.
   133	pub struct MergeBuilder {
   134	    /// The join predicate
   135	    predicate: Expression,
   136	    /// Operations to perform when a source record and target record match
   137	    match_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   138	    /// Operations to perform on source records when they do not pair with a target record
   139	    not_match_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   140	    /// Operations to perform on target records when they do not pair with a source record
   141	    not_match_source_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   142	    ///Prefix the source columns with a user provided prefix
   143	    source_alias: Option<String>,
   144	    ///Prefix target columns with a user provided prefix
   145	    target_alias: Option<String>,
   146	    /// A snapshot of the table's state. AKA the target table in the operation
   147	    snapshot: Option<EagerSnapshot>,
   148	    /// The source data
   149	    source: DataFrame,
   150	    /// Whether the source is a streaming source (if true, stats deducing to prune target is disabled)
   151	    streaming: bool,
   152	    /// Enable merge schema evolution
   153	    merge_schema: bool,
   154	    /// Delta object store for handling data files
   155	    log_store: LogStoreRef,
   156	    /// Datafusion session state relevant for executing the input plan
   157	    state: Option<Arc<dyn Session>>,
   158	    session_fallback_policy: SessionFallbackPolicy,
   159	    /// Properties passed to underlying parquet writer for when files are rewritten
   160	    writer_properties: Option<WriterProperties>,
   161	    /// Additional information to add to the commit
   162	    commit_properties: CommitProperties,
   163	    /// safe_cast determines how data types that do not match the underlying table are handled
   164	    /// By default an error is returned
   165	    safe_cast: bool,
   166	    custom_execute_handler: Option<Arc<dyn CustomExecuteHandler>>,
   167	}
   168	
   169	impl super::Operation for MergeBuilder {
   170	    fn log_store(&self) -> &LogStoreRef {
   171	        &self.log_store
   172	    }
   173	    fn get_custom_execute_handler(&self) -> Option<Arc<dyn CustomExecuteHandler>> {
   174	        self.custom_execute_handler.clone()
   175	    }
   176	}
   177	
   178	impl MergeBuilder {
   179	    /// Create a new [`MergeBuilder`]
   180	    pub fn new<E: Into<Expression>>(
   181	        log_store: LogStoreRef,
   182	        snapshot: Option<EagerSnapshot>,
   183	        predicate: E,
   184	        source: DataFrame,
   185	    ) -> Self {
   186	        let predicate = predicate.into();
   187	        Self {
   188	            predicate,
   189	            source,
   190	            snapshot,
   191	            log_store,
   192	            source_alias: None,
   193	            target_alias: None,
   194	            state: None,
   195	            session_fallback_policy: SessionFallbackPolicy::default(),
   196	            commit_properties: CommitProperties::default(),
   197	            writer_properties: None,
   198	            merge_schema: false,
   199	            match_operations: Vec::new(),
   200	            not_match_operations: Vec::new(),
   201	            not_match_source_operations: Vec::new(),
   202	            safe_cast: false,
   203	            streaming: false,
   204	            custom_execute_handler: None,
   205	        }
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    /// Update a target record when it matches with a source record
   209	    ///
   210	    /// The update expressions can specify both source and target columns.
   211	    ///
   212	    /// Multiple match clauses can be specified and their predicates are
   213	    /// evaluated to determine if the corresponding operation are performed.
   214	    /// Only the first clause that results in a satisfy predicate is executed.
   215	    /// The order of match clauses matter.
   216	    ///
   217	    /// #Example
   218	    /// ```rust ignore
   219	    /// let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;
   220	    /// let (table, metrics) = DeltaOps(table)
   221	    ///     .merge(source, col("target.id").eq(col("source.id")))
   222	    ///     .with_source_alias("source")
   223	    ///     .with_target_alias("target")
   224	    ///     .when_matched_update(|update| {
   225	    ///         update
   226	    ///             .predicate(col("source.value").lt(lit(0)))
   227	    ///             .update("value", lit(0))
   228	    ///             .update("modified", col("source.modified"))
   229	    ///     })?
   230	    ///     .when_matched_update(|update| {
   231	    ///         update
   232	    ///             .update("value", col("source.value") + lit(1))
   233	    ///             .update("modified", col("source.modified"))
   234	    ///     })?
   235	    ///     .await?
   236	    /// ```
   237	    pub fn when_matched_update<F>(mut self, builder: F) -> DeltaResult<MergeBuilder>
   238	    where
   239	        F: FnOnce(UpdateBuilder) -> UpdateBuilder,
   240	    {
   241	        let builder = builder(UpdateBuilder::default());
   242	        let op =
   243	            MergeOperationConfig::new(builder.predicate, builder.updates, OperationType::Update)?;
   244	        self.match_operations.push(op);
   245	        Ok(self)
   246	    }
   247	
   248	    /// Delete a target record when it matches with a source record
   249	    ///
   250	    /// Multiple match clauses can be specified and their predicates are
   251	    /// evaluated to determine if the corresponding operation are performed.
   252	    /// Only the first clause that results in a satisfy predicate is executed.
   253	    /// The order of match clauses matter.
   254	    ///
   255	    /// #Example
   256	    /// ```rust ignore
   257	    /// let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;
   258	    /// let (table, metrics) = DeltaOps(table)
   259	    ///     .merge(source, col("target.id").eq(col("source.id")))
   260	    ///     .with_source_alias("source")
   261	    ///     .with_target_alias("target")
   262	    ///     .when_matched_delete(|delete| {
   263	    ///         delete.predicate(col("source.delete"))
   264	    ///     })?
   265	    ///     .await?
   266	    /// ```
   267	    pub fn when_matched_delete<F>(mut self, builder: F) -> DeltaResult<MergeBuilder>
   268	    where
   269	        F: FnOnce(DeleteBuilder) -> DeleteBuilder,
   270	    {
   271	        let builder = builder(DeleteBuilder::default());
   272	        let op = MergeOperationConfig::new(
   273	            builder.predicate,
   274	            HashMap::default(),
   275	            OperationType::Delete,
   276	        )?;
   277	        self.match_operations.push(op);
   278	        Ok(self)
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    /// Insert a source record when it does not match with a target record
   282	    ///
   283	    /// Multiple not match clauses can be specified and their predicates are
   284	    /// evaluated to determine if the corresponding operation are performed.
   285	    /// Only the first clause that results in a satisfy predicate is executed.
   286	    /// The order of not match clauses matter.
   287	    ///
   288	    /// #Example
   289	    /// ```rust ignore
   290	    /// let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;
   291	    /// let (table, metrics) = DeltaOps(table)
   292	    ///     .merge(source, col("target.id").eq(col("source.id")))
   293	    ///     .with_source_alias("source")
   294	    ///     .with_target_alias("target")
   295	    ///     .when_not_matched_insert(|insert| {
   296	    ///         insert
   297	    ///             .set("id", col("source.id"))
   298	    ///             .set("value", col("source.value"))
   299	    ///             .set("modified", col("source.modified"))
   300	    ///     })?
   301	    ///     .await?
   302	    /// ```
   303	    pub fn when_not_matched_insert<F>(mut self, builder: F) -> DeltaResult<MergeBuilder>
   304	    where
   305	        F: FnOnce(InsertBuilder) -> InsertBuilder,
   306	    {
   307	        let builder = builder(InsertBuilder::default());
   308	        let op = MergeOperationConfig::new(builder.predicate, builder.set, OperationType::Insert)?;
   309	        self.not_match_operations.push(op);
   310	        Ok(self)
   311	    }
   312	
   313	    /// Update a target record when it does not match with a
   314	    /// source record
   315	    ///
   316	    /// The update expressions can specify only target columns.
   317	    ///
   318	    /// Multiple source not match clauses can be specified and their predicates
   319	    /// are evaluated to determine if the corresponding operation are performed.
   320	    /// Only the first clause that results in a satisfy predicate is executed.
   321	    /// The order of source not match clauses matter.
   322	    ///
   323	    /// #Example
   324	    /// ```rust ignore
   325	    /// let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;
   326	    /// let (table, metrics) = DeltaOps(table)
   327	    ///     .merge(source, col("target.id").eq(col("source.id")))
   328	    ///     .with_source_alias("source")
   329	    ///     .with_target_alias("target")
   330	    ///     .when_not_matched_by_source_update(|update| {
   331	    ///         update
   332	    ///             .update("active", lit(false))
   333	    ///             .update("to_dt", lit("2023-07-11"))
   334	    ///     })?
   335	    ///     .await?
   336	    /// ```
   337	    pub fn when_not_matched_by_source_update<F>(mut self, builder: F) -> DeltaResult<MergeBuilder>
   338	    where
   339	        F: FnOnce(UpdateBuilder) -> UpdateBuilder,
   340	    {
   341	        let builder = builder(UpdateBuilder::default());
   342	        let op =
   343	            MergeOperationConfig::new(builder.predicate, builder.updates, OperationType::Update)?;
   344	        self.not_match_source_operations.push(op);
   345	        Ok(self)
   346	    }
   347	
   348	    /// Delete a target record when it does not match with a source record
   349	    ///
   350	    /// Multiple source "not match" clauses can be specified and their predicates
   351	    /// are evaluated to determine if the corresponding operations are performed.
   352	    /// Only the first clause that results in a satisfy predicate is executed.
   353	    /// The order of source "not match" clauses matter.
   354	    ///
   355	    /// #Example
   356	    /// ```rust ignore
   357	    /// let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;

   362	    ///     .when_not_matched_by_source_delete(|delete| {
   363	    ///         delete
   364	    ///     })?
   365	    ///     .await?
   366	    /// ```
   367	    pub fn when_not_matched_by_source_delete<F>(mut self, builder: F) -> DeltaResult<MergeBuilder>
   368	    where
   369	        F: FnOnce(DeleteBuilder) -> DeleteBuilder,
   370	    {
   371	        let builder = builder(DeleteBuilder::default());
   372	        let op = MergeOperationConfig::new(
   373	            builder.predicate,
   374	            HashMap::default(),
   375	            OperationType::Delete,
   376	        )?;
   377	        self.not_match_source_operations.push(op);
   378	        Ok(self)
   379	    }

   460	/// Builder for update clauses
   461	pub struct UpdateBuilder {
   462	    /// Only update records that match the predicate
   463	    predicate: Option<Expression>,
   464	    /// How to update columns in the target table
   465	    updates: HashMap<Column, Expression>,

   473	    }

   475	    /// How a column from the target table should be updated.
   476	    /// In the match case the expression may contain both source and target columns.
   477	    /// In the source not match case the expression may only contain target columns
   478	    pub fn update<C: Into<DeltaColumn>, E: Into<Expression>>(
   479	        mut self,
   480	        column: C,
   481	        expression: E,
   482	    ) -> Self {
   483	        self.updates.insert(column.into().into(), expression.into());
   484	        self
   485	    }
   486	}

   539	//Encapsute the User's Merge configuration for later processing
   540	struct MergeOperationConfig {
   541	    /// Which records to update
   542	    predicate: Option<Expression>,
   543	    /// How to update columns in a record that match the predicate
   544	    operations: HashMap<Column, Expression>,
   545	    r#type: OperationType,

   548	struct MergeOperation {
   549	    /// Which records to update
   550	    predicate: Option<Expr>,
   551	    /// How to update columns in a record that match the predicate
   552	    operations: HashMap<Column, Expr>,
   553	    r#type: OperationType,
   554	}
   555	
   556	impl MergeOperation {
   557	    fn try_from(
   558	        config: MergeOperationConfig,
   559	        schema: &DFSchema,
   560	        state: &dyn Session,
   561	        target_alias: &Option<String>,
   562	    ) -> DeltaResult<MergeOperation> {
   563	        let mut ops = HashMap::with_capacity(config.operations.capacity());
   564	
   565	        for (column, expression) in config.operations.into_iter() {
   566	            // Normalize the column name to contain the target alias. If a table reference was provided ensure it's the target.
   567	            let column = match target_alias {
   568	                Some(alias) => {
   569	                    let r = TableReference::bare(alias.to_owned());
   570	                    match column {
   571	                        Column {
   572	                            relation: None,
   573	                            name,
   574	                            spans,
   575	                        } => Column {
   576	                            relation: Some(r),
   577	                            name,
   578	                            spans,
   579	                        },
   580	                        Column {
   581	                            relation: Some(TableReference::Bare { table }),
   582	                            name,
   583	                            spans,
   584	                        } => {
   585	                            if table.as_ref() == alias {
   586	                                Column {
   587	                                    relation: Some(r),
   588	                                    name,
   589	                                    spans,
   590	                                }
   591	                            } else {
   592	                                return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic(format!(
   593	                                    "Table alias '{table}' in column reference '{table}.{name}' unknown. Hint: You must reference the Delta Table with alias '{alias}'."
   594	                                )));
   595	                            }
   596	                        }
   597	                        _ => {
   598	                            return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic(
   599	                                "Column must reference column in Delta table".into(),
   600	                            ));

   607	        }
   608	
   609	        Ok(MergeOperation {
   610	            predicate: maybe_into_expr(config.predicate, schema, state)?,
   611	            operations: ops,
   612	            r#type: config.r#type,
   613	        })
   614	    }
   615	}
   616	
   617	impl MergeOperationConfig {
   618	    pub fn new(
   619	        predicate: Option<Expression>,
   620	        operations: HashMap<Column, Expression>,
   621	        r#type: OperationType,
   622	    ) -> DeltaResult<Self> {
   623	        Ok(MergeOperationConfig {
   624	            predicate,
   625	            operations,
   626	            r#type,
   627	        })
   628	    }
   629	}
   630	
   631	#[derive(Default, Serialize, Debug)]
   632	/// Metrics for the Merge Operation
   633	pub struct MergeMetrics {
   634	    /// Number of rows in the source data
   635	    pub num_source_rows: usize,
   636	    /// Number of rows inserted into the target table
   637	    pub num_target_rows_inserted: usize,
   638	    /// Number of rows updated in the target table
   639	    pub num_target_rows_updated: usize,
   640	    /// Number of rows deleted in the target table
   641	    pub num_target_rows_deleted: usize,
   642	    /// Number of target rows copied
   643	    pub num_target_rows_copied: usize,
   644	    /// Total number of rows written out
   645	    pub num_output_rows: usize,
   646	    /// Amount of files considered during table scan
   647	    pub num_target_files_scanned: usize,
   648	    /// Amount of files not considered (pruned) during table scan
   649	    pub num_target_files_skipped_during_scan: usize,
   650	    /// Number of files added to the sink(target)
   651	    pub num_target_files_added: usize,
   652	    /// Number of files removed from the sink(target)
   653	    pub num_target_files_removed: usize,
   654	    /// Time taken to execute the entire operation
   655	    pub execution_time_ms: u64,
   656	    /// Time taken to scan the files for matches
   657	    pub scan_time_ms: u64,
   658	    /// Time taken to rewrite the matched files
   659	    pub rewrite_time_ms: u64,
   660	}
   661	#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
   662	pub(crate) struct MergeMetricExtensionPlanner {}
   663	
   664	impl MergeMetricExtensionPlanner {
   665	    pub fn new() -> Arc<Self> {
   666	        Arc::new(Self {})
   667	    }
   668	}
   669	
   670	#[async_trait]
   671	impl ExtensionPlanner for MergeMetricExtensionPlanner {
   672	    async fn plan_extension(
   673	        &self,
   674	        planner: &dyn PhysicalPlanner,
   675	        node: &dyn UserDefinedLogicalNode,
   676	        _logical_inputs: &[&LogicalPlan],
   677	        physical_inputs: &[Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>],
   678	        session_state: &SessionState,
   679	    ) -> DataFusionResult<Option<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>>> {
   680	        if let Some(metric_observer) = node.as_any().downcast_ref::<MetricObserver>() {
   681	            if metric_observer.id.eq(SOURCE_COUNT_ID) {
   682	                return Ok(Some(MetricObserverExec::try_new(
   683	                    SOURCE_COUNT_ID.into(),
   684	                    physical_inputs,
   685	                    |batch, metrics| {
   686	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   687	                            .global_counter(SOURCE_COUNT_METRIC)
   688	                            .add(batch.num_rows());
   689	                    },
   690	                )?));
   691	            }
   692	
   693	            if metric_observer.id.eq(TARGET_COUNT_ID) {
   694	                return Ok(Some(MetricObserverExec::try_new(
   695	                    TARGET_COUNT_ID.into(),
   696	                    physical_inputs,
   697	                    |batch, metrics| {
   698	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   699	                            .global_counter(TARGET_COUNT_METRIC)
   700	                            .add(batch.num_rows());
   701	                    },
   702	                )?));
   703	            }
   704	
   705	            if metric_observer.id.eq(OUTPUT_COUNT_ID) {
   706	                return Ok(Some(MetricObserverExec::try_new(
   707	                    OUTPUT_COUNT_ID.into(),
   708	                    physical_inputs,
   709	                    |batch, metrics| {
   710	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   711	                            .global_counter(TARGET_INSERTED_METRIC)
   712	                            .add(
   713	                                batch
   714	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN)
   715	                                    .unwrap()
   716	                                    .null_count(),
   717	                            );
   718	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   719	                            .global_counter(TARGET_UPDATED_METRIC)
   720	                            .add(
   721	                                batch
   722	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN)
   723	                                    .unwrap()
   724	                                    .null_count(),
   725	                            );
   726	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   727	                            .global_counter(TARGET_DELETED_METRIC)
   728	                            .add(
   729	                                batch
   730	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN)
   731	                                    .unwrap()
   732	                                    .null_count(),
   733	                            );
   734	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   735	                            .global_counter(TARGET_COPY_METRIC)
   736	                            .add(
   737	                                batch
   738	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_COPY_COLUMN)
   739	                                    .unwrap()
   740	                                    .null_count(),
   741	                            );
   742	                    },
   743	                )?));
   744	            }
   745	        }
   746	
   747	        if let Some(barrier) = node.as_any().downcast_ref::<MergeBarrier>() {
   748	            if physical_inputs.len() != 1 {
   749	                return plan_err!("MergeBarrierExec expects exactly one input");
   750	            }
   751	            let schema = barrier.input.schema();
   752	            return Ok(Some(Arc::new(MergeBarrierExec::new(
   753	                physical_inputs.first().unwrap().clone(),
   754	                barrier.file_column.clone(),
   755	                planner.create_physical_expr(&barrier.expr, schema, session_state)?,
   756	            ))));
   757	        }
   758	
   759	        Ok(None)
   760	    }
   761	}
   762	
   763	#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
   764	#[tracing::instrument(skip_all, fields(operation = "merge", version = snapshot.version(), table_uri = %log_store.root_url()))]
   765	async fn execute(
   766	    predicate: Expression,
   767	    mut source: DataFrame,
   768	    log_store: LogStoreRef,
   769	    snapshot: EagerSnapshot,
   770	    state: SessionState,
   771	    writer_properties: Option<WriterProperties>,
   772	    mut commit_properties: CommitProperties,
   773	    _safe_cast: bool,
   774	    streaming: bool,
   775	    source_alias: Option<String>,
   776	    target_alias: Option<String>,
   777	    merge_schema: bool,
   778	    match_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   779	    not_match_target_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   780	    not_match_source_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   781	    operation_id: Uuid,
   782	    handle: Option<&Arc<dyn CustomExecuteHandler>>,
   783	) -> DeltaResult<(EagerSnapshot, MergeMetrics)> {
   784	    info!(
   785	        operation = "merge",
   786	        version = snapshot.version(),
   787	        "starting merge execution"
   788	    );
   789	
   790	    let mut metrics = MergeMetrics::default();
   791	    let exec_start = Instant::now();
   792	    // Determining whether we should write change data once so that computation of change data can
   793	    // be disabled in the common case(s)
   794	    let should_cdc = should_write_cdc(&snapshot)?;
   795	    // Change data may be collected and then written out at the completion of the merge
   796	
   797	    if should_cdc {
   798	        debug!("Executing a merge and I should write CDC!");
   799	    }
   800	
   801	    info!(cdc_enabled = should_cdc, "merge execution details");
   802	
   803	    let current_metadata = snapshot.metadata();
   804	    let merge_planner = DeltaPlanner::new();
   805	
   806	    let state = SessionStateBuilder::new_from_existing(state)
   807	        .with_query_planner(merge_planner)
   808	        .build();
   809	
   810	    // TODO: Given the join predicate, remove any expression that involve the
   811	    // source table and keep expressions that only involve the target table.
   812	    // This would allow us to perform statistics/partition pruning E.G
   813	    // Expression source.id = id and to_dt = '9999-12-31' -Becomes-> to_dt =
   814	    // '9999-12-31'
   815	    //
   816	    // If the user specified any not_source_match operations then those
   817	    // predicates also need to be considered when pruning
   818	
   819	    let source_name = match &source_alias {
   820	        Some(alias) => TableReference::bare(alias.to_string()),
   821	        None => TableReference::bare(UNNAMED_TABLE),
   822	    };
   823	
   824	    let target_name = match &target_alias {
   825	        Some(alias) => TableReference::bare(alias.to_string()),
   826	        None => TableReference::bare(UNNAMED_TABLE),
   827	    };
   828	
   829	    let mut generated_col_exp = None;
   830	    let mut missing_generated_col = None;
   831	
   832	    if gc_is_enabled(&snapshot) {
   833	        let generated_col_expressions = snapshot.schema().get_generated_columns()?;
   834	        let (source_with_gc, missing_generated_columns) =
   835	            add_missing_generated_columns(source, &generated_col_expressions)?;
   836	
   837	        source = source_with_gc;
   838	        generated_col_exp = Some(generated_col_expressions);
   839	        missing_generated_col = Some(missing_generated_columns);
   840	    }
   841	    // This is only done to provide the source columns with a correct table reference. Just renaming the columns does not work
   842	    let source = LogicalPlanBuilder::scan(
   843	        source_name.clone(),
   844	        provider_as_source(source.into_view()),
   845	        None,
   846	    )?
   847	    .build()?;
   848	
   849	    let source = LogicalPlan::Extension(Extension {
   850	        node: Arc::new(MetricObserver {
   851	            id: SOURCE_COUNT_ID.into(),
   852	            input: source,
   853	            enable_pushdown: false,
   854	        }),
   855	    });
   856	
   857	    let file_column = Arc::new(resolve_file_column_name(
   858	        snapshot.input_schema().as_ref(),
   859	        None,
   860	    )?);
   861	
   862	    let target_provider = provider_as_source(
   863	        DeltaScanNext::builder()
   864	            .with_eager_snapshot(snapshot.clone())
   865	            .with_log_store(log_store.clone())
   866	            .with_file_column(file_column.as_str())
   867	            .await?,
   868	    );
   869	    let target =
   870	        LogicalPlanBuilder::scan(target_name.clone(), target_provider.clone(), None)?.build()?;
   871	
   872	    let source_schema = source.schema();
   873	    let target_schema = target.schema();
   874	
   875	    let join_schema_df = build_join_schema(source_schema, target_schema, &JoinType::Full)?;
   876	
   877	    let predicate = predicate.resolve(&state, Arc::new(join_schema_df.clone()))?;
   878	
   879	    // Attempt to construct an early filter that we can apply to the Add action list and the delta scan.
   880	    // In the case where there are partition columns in the join predicate, we can scan the source table
   881	    // to get the distinct list of partitions affected and constrain the search to those.
   882	
   883	    let target_subset_filter: Option<Expr> = if !not_match_source_operations.is_empty() {
   884	        // It's only worth trying to create an early filter where there are no `when_not_matched_source` operators, since
   885	        // that implies a full scan
   886	        None
   887	    } else {
   888	        try_construct_early_filter(
   889	            predicate.clone(),
   890	            &snapshot,
   891	            &state,
   892	            &source,
   893	            &source_name,
   894	            &target_name,
   895	            streaming,
   896	        )
   897	        .await?
   898	    }
   899	    .map(|e| normalize_target_subset_filter(target.schema().clone(), e))
   900	    .transpose()?;

  1038	    fn update_case(
  1039	        operations: Vec<MergeOperation>,
  1040	        ops: &mut Vec<(HashMap<Column, Expr>, OperationType)>,
  1041	        when_expr: &mut Vec<Expr>,
  1042	        then_expr: &mut Vec<Expr>,
  1043	        base_expr: &Expr,
  1044	    ) -> DeltaResult<Vec<MergePredicate>> {
  1045	        let mut predicates = Vec::with_capacity(operations.len());
  1046	
  1047	        for op in operations {
  1048	            let predicate = match &op.predicate {
  1049	                Some(predicate) => base_expr.clone().and(predicate.to_owned()),
  1050	                None => base_expr.clone(),
  1051	            };
  1052	
  1053	            when_expr.push(predicate);
  1054	            then_expr.push(lit(ops.len() as i32));
  1055	
  1056	            ops.push((op.operations, op.r#type));
  1057	
  1058	            let action_type = match op.r#type {
  1059	                OperationType::Update => "update",
  1060	                OperationType::Delete => "delete",
  1061	                OperationType::Insert => "insert",
  1062	                OperationType::SourceDelete => {
  1063	                    return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic("Invalid action type".to_string()));
  1064	                }
  1065	                OperationType::Copy => {
  1066	                    return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic("Invalid action type".to_string()));
  1067	                }
  1068	            };
  1069	
  1070	            let action_type = action_type.to_string();
  1071	            let predicate = op
  1072	                .predicate
  1073	                .map(|expr| fmt_expr_to_sql(&expr))
  1074	                .transpose()?;
  1075	
  1076	            predicates.push(MergePredicate {
  1077	                action_type,
  1078	                predicate,
  1079	            });
  1080	        }
  1081	        Ok(predicates)
  1082	    }
  1083	
  1084	    let match_operations = update_case(
  1085	        match_operations,
  1086	        &mut ops,
  1087	        &mut when_expr,
  1088	        &mut then_expr,
  1089	        &matched,
  1090	    )?;
  1091

  1105	        &not_matched_source,
  1106	    )?;
  1107

  1520	    metrics.execution_time_ms = Instant::now().duration_since(exec_start).as_millis() as u64;
  1521	
  1522	    let app_metadata = &mut commit_properties.app_metadata;
  1523	    app_metadata.insert("readVersion".to_owned(), snapshot.version().into());
  1524	    if let Ok(map) = serde_json::to_value(&metrics) {
  1525	        app_metadata.insert("operationMetrics".to_owned(), map);
  1526	    }
  1527	
  1528	    // Do not make a commit when there are zero updates to the state
  1529	    let operation = DeltaOperation::Merge {
  1530	        predicate: commit_predicate,
  1531	        merge_predicate: Some(fmt_expr_to_sql(&predicate)?),
  1532	        matched_predicates: match_operations,
  1533	        not_matched_predicates: not_match_target_operations,
  1534	        not_matched_by_source_predicates: not_match_source_operations,
  1535	    };
  1536	
  1537	    if actions.is_empty() {
  1538	        return Ok((snapshot, metrics));
  1539	    }
  1540	
  1541	    let commit = CommitBuilder::from(commit_properties)
  1542	        .with_actions(actions)
  1543	        .with_operation_id(operation_id)
  1544	        .with_post_commit_hook_handler(handle.cloned())
  1545	        .build(Some(&snapshot), log_store.clone(), operation)
  1546	        .await?;
  1547	    Ok((commit.snapshot().snapshot, metrics))
  1548	}
  1549	
  1550	fn modify_schema(
  1551	    ending_schema: &mut SchemaBuilder,
  1552	    target_schema: &DFSchema,
  1553	    source_schema: &DFSchema,
  1554	    operations: &[MergeOperation],
  1555	) -> DeltaResult<()> {
  1556	    for columns in operations
  1557	        .iter()
  1558	        .filter(|ops| matches!(ops.r#type, OperationType::Update | OperationType::Insert))
  1559	        .flat_map(|ops| ops.operations.keys())
  1560	    {
  1561	        // This assume that all the columns in the MERGE operations of UPDATE and INSERT at least exists in the source table
  1562	        let source_field = source_schema.field_with_unqualified_name(columns.name())?;
  1563	        if source_field
  1564	            .metadata()
  1565	            .contains_key(ColumnMetadataKey::GenerationExpression.as_ref())
  1566	        {
  1567	            let error = arrow::error::ArrowError::SchemaError("Schema evolved fields cannot have generated expressions. Recreate the table to achieve this.".to_string());
  1568	            return Err(DeltaTableError::Arrow { source: error });
  1569	        }
  1570	        //Check if the columns in the source schema exist in the target schema
  1571	        match target_schema.field_from_column(columns) {
  1572	            Ok(target_field) => {
  1573	                // This case is when there is an added column in an nested datatype
  1574	                let new_field = merge_arrow_field(target_field, source_field, true)?;
  1575	                if new_field != **target_field {
  1576	                    ending_schema.try_merge(&Arc::new(new_field))?;
  1577	                }
  1578	            }
  1579	            Err(_) => {
  1580	                // This function is called multiple time with different operations so this handle any collisions
  1581	                ending_schema
  1582	                    .try_merge(&Arc::new(source_field.as_ref().clone().with_nullable(true)))?;
  1583	            }
  1584	        }
  1585	    }
  1586	    Ok(())
  1587	}
  1588	
  1589	fn remove_table_alias(expr: Expr, table_alias: &str) -> Expr {
  1590	    expr.transform(&|expr| match expr {
  1591	        Expr::Column(c) => match c.relation {
  1592	            Some(rel) if rel.table() == table_alias => Ok(Transformed::yes(Expr::Column(
  1593	                Column::new_unqualified(c.name),
  1594	            ))),
  1595	            _ => Ok(Transformed::no(Expr::Column(Column::new(
  1596	                c.relation, c.name,
  1597	            )))),
  1598	        },
  1599	        _ => Ok(Transformed::no(expr)),
  1600	    })
  1601	    .unwrap()
  1602	    .data
  1603	}
  1604	
  1605	fn normalize_target_subset_filter(target_schema: DFSchemaRef, expr: Expr) -> DeltaResult<Expr> {
  1606	    let expr = coerce_predicate_literals(expr, target_schema.as_ref())?;
  1607	    let props = ExecutionProps::new();
  1608	    let simplify_context = SimplifyContext::new(&props).with_schema(target_schema);
  1609	    let simplifier = ExprSimplifier::new(simplify_context).with_max_cycles(10);
  1610	    Ok(simplifier.simplify(expr)?)
  1611	}
  1612	
  1613	fn build_file_skipping_predicates(
  1614	    target_subset_filter: Option<Expr>,
  1615	    target_alias: Option<&str>,
  1616	) -> Vec<Expr> {
  1617	    let Some(filter) = target_subset_filter else {
  1618	        return Vec::new();
  1619	    };
  1620	
  1621	    // Strip the target alias before binding scan predicates.
  1622	    let filter = match target_alias {
  1623	        Some(alias) => remove_table_alias(filter, alias),
  1624	        None => filter,
  1625	    };
  1626	
  1627	    split_conjunction_owned(filter)
  1628	}
  1629	
  1630	fn derive_skipped_file_count(total_files: usize, scanned_files: usize) -> (usize, bool) {
  1631	    let impossible_state = scanned_files > total_files;
  1632	    (total_files.saturating_sub(scanned_files), impossible_state)
  1633	}
  1634	
  1635	fn get_metric_any(metrics: &MetricsSet, names: &[&str]) -> Option<usize> {
  1636	    names
  1637	        .iter()
  1638	        .find_map(|name| metrics.sum_by_name(name).map(|metric| metric.as_usize()))
  1639	}
  1640	
  1641	fn get_metric_any_or(
  1642	    metrics: &MetricsSet,
  1643	    names: &[&str],
  1644	    fallback: impl FnOnce() -> usize,
  1645	) -> usize {
  1646	    get_metric_any(metrics, names).unwrap_or_else(fallback)
  1647	}
  1648	
  1649	fn should_remove_rewritten_file(
  1650	    survivors: &barrier::BarrierSurvivorSet,
  1651	    rel_path: &str,
  1652	    table_root: &url::Url,
  1653	) -> DeltaResult<bool> {
  1654	    if survivors.contains(rel_path) {
  1655	        return Ok(true);
  1656	    }
  1657	
  1658	    // Compare against normalized file IDs.
  1659	    let full_id = normalize_path_as_file_id(rel_path, table_root, "merge remove")?;
  1660	    Ok(survivors.contains(full_id.as_str()))
  1661	}
  1662	impl std::future::IntoFuture for MergeBuilder {

  1679	                this.state.as_deref(),

     1	//! Merge Barrier determines which files have modifications during the merge operation
     2	//!
     3	//! For every unique path in the input stream, a barrier is established. If any
     4	//! single record for a file contains any delete, update, or insert operations
     5	//! then the barrier for the file is opened and can be sent downstream.
     6	//! To determine if a file contains zero changes, the input stream is
     7	//! exhausted. Afterwards, records are then dropped.
     8	//!
     9	//! Bookkeeping is maintained to determine which files have modifications, so
    10	//! they can be removed from the delta log.
    11

    42	pub struct MergeBarrierExec {

    96	        self: Arc<Self>,

    99	        if children.len() != 1 {
   100	            return Err(DataFusionError::Plan(
   101	                "MergeBarrierExec wrong number of children".to_string(),
   102	            ));
   103	        }
   104	        Ok(Arc::new(MergeBarrierExec::new(
   105	            children[0].clone(),
   106	            self.file_column.clone(),
   107	            self.expr.clone(),

   109	    }

   115	    ) -> datafusion::common::Result<datafusion::physical_plan::SendableRecordBatchStream> {
   116	        let input = self.input.execute(partition, context)?;

   138	
   139	#[derive(Debug)]
   140	enum State {
   141	    Feed,
   142	    Drain,
   143	    Finalize,
   144	    Abort,
   145	    Done,
   146	}
   147	
   148	#[derive(Debug)]
   149	enum PartitionBarrierState {
   150	    Closed,
   151	    Open,
   152	}
   153	
   154	#[derive(Debug)]
   155	struct MergeBarrierPartition {
   156	    state: PartitionBarrierState,
   157	    buffer: Vec<RecordBatch>,
   158	    file_name: Option<String>,
   159	}
   160	
   161	impl MergeBarrierPartition {
   162	    pub fn new(file_name: Option<String>) -> Self {
   163	        MergeBarrierPartition {
   164	            state: PartitionBarrierState::Closed,
   165	            buffer: Vec::new(),
   166	            file_name,
   167	        }
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    pub fn feed(&mut self, batch: RecordBatch) -> DataFusionResult<()> {
   171	        match self.state {
   172	            PartitionBarrierState::Closed => {
   173	                let delete_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN)?;
   174	                let update_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN)?;
   175	                let insert_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN)?;
   176	                self.buffer.push(batch);
   177	
   178	                if insert_count > 0 || update_count > 0 || delete_count > 0 {
   179	                    self.state = PartitionBarrierState::Open;
   180	                }
   181	            }
   182	            PartitionBarrierState::Open => {
   183	                self.buffer.push(batch);
   184	            }
   185	        }
   186	        Ok(())
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    pub fn drain(&mut self) -> Option<RecordBatch> {
   190	        match self.state {
   191	            PartitionBarrierState::Closed => None,
   192	            PartitionBarrierState::Open => self.buffer.pop(),
   193	        }
   194	    }
   195	}
   196	
   197	struct MergeBarrierStream {
   198	    schema: SchemaRef,
   199	    state: State,
   200	    input: SendableRecordBatchStream,
   201	    file_column: Arc<String>,
   202	    survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
   203	    map: HashMap<String, usize>,
   204	    file_partitions: Vec<MergeBarrierPartition>,
   205	}
   206	
   207	impl MergeBarrierStream {
   208	    pub fn new(
   209	        input: SendableRecordBatchStream,
   210	        schema: SchemaRef,
   211	        survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
   212	        file_column: Arc<String>,
   213	    ) -> Self {
   214	        // Always allocate for a null bucket at index 0;
   215	        let file_partitions = vec![MergeBarrierPartition::new(None)];
   216	
   217	        MergeBarrierStream {
   218	            schema,
   219	            state: State::Feed,
   220	            input,
   221	            file_column,
   222	            survivors,
   223	            file_partitions,
   224	            map: HashMap::new(),
   225	        }
   226	    }
   227	}
   228	
   229	fn get_count(batch: &RecordBatch, column: &str) -> DataFusionResult<usize> {
   230	    batch
   231	        .column_by_name(column)
   232	        .map(|array| array.null_count())
   233	        .ok_or_else(|| {
   234	            DataFusionError::External(Box::new(DeltaTableError::Generic(
   235	                "Required operation column is missing".to_string(),
   236	            )))
   237	        })
   238	}
   239	
   240	impl Stream for MergeBarrierStream {
   241	    type Item = DataFusionResult<RecordBatch>;
   242	
   243	    fn poll_next(mut self: Pin<&mut Self>, cx: &mut Context<'_>) -> Poll<Option<Self::Item>> {
   244	        loop {
   245	            match self.state {
   246	                State::Feed => {
   247	                    match self.input.poll_next_unpin(cx) {
   248	                        Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch))) => {
   249	                            let file_dictionary = get_path_column(&batch, &self.file_column)?;
   250	
   251	                            // For each record batch, the key for a file path is not stable.
   252	                            // We can iterate through the dictionary and lookup the correspond string for each record and then lookup the correct `file_partition` for that value.
   253	                            // However this approach exposes the cost of hashing so we want to minimize that as much as possible.
   254	                            // A map from an arrow dictionary key to the correct index of `file_partition` is created for each batch that's processed.
   255	                            // This ensures we only need to hash each file path at most once per batch.
   256	                            let mut key_map = Vec::with_capacity(file_dictionary.len());
   257	
   258	                            for file_name in file_dictionary.values().into_iter() {
   259	                                let key = match file_name {
   260	                                    Some(name) => {
   261	                                        if !self.map.contains_key(name) {
   262	                                            let key = self.file_partitions.len();
   263	                                            let part_stream =
   264	                                                MergeBarrierPartition::new(Some(name.to_string()));
   265	                                            self.file_partitions.push(part_stream);
   266	                                            self.map.insert(name.to_string(), key);
   267	                                        }
   268	                                        // Safe unwrap due to the above
   269	                                        *self.map.get(name).unwrap()
   270	                                    }
   271	                                    None => 0,
   272	                                };
   273	                                key_map.push(key)
   274	                            }
   275	
   276	                            let mut indices: Vec<_> =
   277	                                Vec::with_capacity(self.file_partitions.len());
   278	                            for _ in 0..self.file_partitions.len() {
   279	                                indices.push(UInt64Builder::with_capacity(batch.num_rows()));
   280	                            }
   281	
   282	                            for (idx, key) in file_dictionary.keys().iter().enumerate() {
   283	                                match key {
   284	                                    Some(value) => {
   285	                                        indices[key_map[value as usize]].append_value(idx as u64)
   286	                                    }
   287	                                    None => indices[0].append_value(idx as u64),
   288	                                }
   289	                            }
   290	
   291	                            let batches: Vec<Result<(usize, RecordBatch), DataFusionError>> =
   292	                                indices
   293	                                    .into_iter()
   294	                                    .enumerate()
   295	                                    .filter_map(|(partition, mut indices)| {
   296	                                        let indices = indices.finish();
   297	                                        (!indices.is_empty()).then_some((partition, indices))
   298	                                    })
   299	                                    .map(move |(partition, indices)| {
   300	                                        // Produce batches based on indices
   301	                                        let columns = batch
   302	                                            .columns()
   303	                                            .iter()
   304	                                            .map(|c| {
   305	                                                Ok(arrow::compute::take(
   306	                                                    c.as_ref(),
   307	                                                    &indices,
   308	                                                    None,
   309	                                                )?)
   310	                                            })
   311	                                            .collect::<DataFusionResult<Vec<ArrayRef>>>()?;
   312	
   313	                                        // This unwrap is safe since the processed batched has the same schema
   314	                                        let batch =
   315	                                            RecordBatch::try_new(batch.schema(), columns).unwrap();
   316	
   317	                                        Ok((partition, batch))
   318	                                    })
   319	                                    .collect();
   320	
   321	                            for batch in batches {
   322	                                match batch {
   323	                                    Ok((partition, batch)) => {
   324	                                        self.file_partitions[partition].feed(batch)?;
   325	                                    }
   326	                                    Err(err) => {
   327	                                        self.state = State::Abort;
   328	                                        return Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err)));
   329	                                    }
   330	                                }
   331	                            }
   332	
   333	                            self.state = State::Drain;
   334	                            continue;
   335	                        }
   336	                        Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err))) => {
   337	                            self.state = State::Abort;
   338	                            return Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err)));
   339	                        }
   340	                        Poll::Ready(None) => {
   341	                            self.state = State::Finalize;
   342	                            continue;
   343	                        }
   344	                        Poll::Pending => return Poll::Pending,
   345	                    }
   346	                }
   347	                State::Drain => {
   348	                    for part in &mut self.file_partitions {
   349	                        if let Some(batch) = part.drain() {
   350	                            return Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch)));
   351	                        }
   352	                    }
   353	
   354	                    self.state = State::Feed;
   355	                    continue;
   356	                }
   357	                State::Finalize => {
   358	                    for part in &mut self.file_partitions {
   359	                        if let Some(batch) = part.drain() {
   360	                            return Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch)));
   361	                        }
   362	                    }
   363	
   364	                    {
   365	                        for part in &self.file_partitions {
   366	                            match part.state {
   367	                                PartitionBarrierState::Closed => {}
   368	                                PartitionBarrierState::Open => {
   369	                                    if let Some(file_name) = &part.file_name {
   370	                                        self.survivors.insert(file_name.to_owned());
   371	                                    }
   372	                                }
   373	                            }
   374	                        }
   375	                    }
   376	
   377	                    self.state = State::Done;
   378	                    continue;
   379	                }
   380	                State::Abort => return Poll::Ready(None),
   381	                State::Done => return Poll::Ready(None),
   382	            }
   383	        }
   384	    }
   385	
   386	    fn size_hint(&self) -> (usize, Option<usize>) {
   387	        (0, self.input.size_hint().1)
   388	    }
   389	}
   390	
   391	impl RecordBatchStream for MergeBarrierStream {
   392	    fn schema(&self) -> SchemaRef {
   393	        self.schema.clone()
   394	    }
   395	}
   396	
   397	#[derive(Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq, PartialOrd)]
   398	pub(crate) struct MergeBarrier {
   399	    pub input: LogicalPlan,
   400	    pub expr: Expr,
   401	    pub file_column: Arc<String>,
   402	}
   403	
   404	impl UserDefinedLogicalNodeCore for MergeBarrier {
   405	    fn name(&self) -> &str {
   406	        "MergeBarrier"
   407	    }
   408	
   409	    fn inputs(&self) -> Vec<&datafusion::logical_expr::LogicalPlan> {
   410	        vec![&self.input]
   411	    }
   412	
   413	    fn schema(&self) -> &datafusion::common::DFSchemaRef {
   414	        self.input.schema()
   415	    }
   416	
   417	    fn expressions(&self) -> Vec<datafusion::logical_expr::Expr> {
   418	        vec![self.expr.clone()]
   419	    }
   420	
   421	    fn fmt_for_explain(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter) -> std::fmt::Result {
   422	        write!(f, "MergeBarrier")
   423	    }
   424	
   425	    fn with_exprs_and_inputs(
   426	        &self,
   427	        exprs: Vec<datafusion::logical_expr::Expr>,
   428	        inputs: Vec<datafusion::logical_expr::LogicalPlan>,
   429	    ) -> DataFusionResult<Self> {
   430	        Ok(MergeBarrier {
   431	            input: inputs[0].clone(),
   432	            file_column: self.file_column.clone(),
   433	            expr: exprs[0].clone(),
   434	        })
   435	    }
   436	}

   117	async fn merge(
   118	    table: DeltaTable,
   119	    df: DataFrame,
   120	    predicate: Expr,
   121	) -> DeltaResult<(DeltaTable, MergeMetrics)> {
   122	    table
   123	        .merge(df, predicate)
   124	        .with_source_alias("source")
   125	        .with_target_alias("target")
   126	        .when_matched_update(|update| {
   127	            update
   128	                .update("value", col("source.value"))
   129	                .update("event_date", col("source.event_date"))
   130	        })
   131	        .unwrap()
   132	        .when_not_matched_insert(|insert| {
   133	            insert
   134	                .set("id", col("source.id"))
   135	                .set("value", col("source.value"))
   136	                .set("event_date", col("source.event_date"))
   137	        })
   138	        .unwrap()
   139	        .await
   140	}

   142	#[tokio::test]
   143	async fn test_merge_concurrent_conflict() {
   144	    // Overlapping id ranges -> Commit conflict
   145	    let tmp_dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
   146	    let table_uri = tmp_dir.path().to_str().to_owned().unwrap();
   147	
   148	    let table_ref1 = create_table(table_uri, Some(vec!["event_date"])).await;
   149	    let table_url = Url::from_directory_path(table_uri).unwrap();
   150	    let table_ref2 = open_table(table_url).await.unwrap();
   151	    let (df1, _df2) = create_test_data();
   152	
   153	    let expr = col("target.id").eq(col("source.id"));
   154	    let (_table_ref1, _metrics) = merge(table_ref1, df1.clone(), expr.clone()).await.unwrap();
   155	    let result = merge(table_ref2, df1, expr).await;
   156	
   157	    assert!(matches!(
   158	        result.as_ref().unwrap_err(),
   159	        DeltaTableError::Transaction { .. }
   160	    ));
   161	    if let DeltaTableError::Transaction { source } = result.unwrap_err() {
   162	        assert!(matches!(source, TransactionError::CommitConflict(_)));
   163	    }
   164	}

Now let me understand the problem better. The PR description says that when multiple source rows match a single target row, the merge should throw an error rather than inserting new records. Let me search for how the merge handles this.

Looking at the code, the key is in the join: a full outer join is performed. If multiple source rows match the same target row, the join will produce multiple rows for that target row. The current code then processes these as matched rows (both `SOURCE_COLUMN` and `TARGET_COLUMN` are true), which would cause multiple updates for the same target row, effectively duplicating it.

The fix should detect that there are multiple source rows matching a single target row and raise an error. Let me look at how Spark/Databricks handles this - they typically raise an error like "Multiple source rows matched the same target row".

Let me look at how the match is detected:

Now I understand. The merge does a full outer join, and each row gets tagged with SOURCE_COLUMN and TARGET_COLUMN to indicate whether it came from source or target. If multiple source rows join to one target row, we'd get multiple rows where both SOURCE_COLUMN and TARGET_COLUMN are true for the same target row.

The issue is that the merge should validate that there's at most one source row per target row for the matched case (when_matched_update), and raise an error otherwise.

    29	pub(crate) struct PyMergeBuilder {
    30	    _builder: Option<MergeBuilder>,
    31	    #[pyo3(get)]
    32	    source_alias: Option<String>,
    33	    #[pyo3(get)]
    34	    target_alias: Option<String>,
    35	    #[pyo3(get)]
    36	    merge_schema: bool,
    37	    arrow_schema: Arc<ArrowSchema>,

    39	
    40	impl PyMergeBuilder {
    41	    #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
    42	    pub fn new(
    43	        log_store: LogStoreRef,
    44	        snapshot: EagerSnapshot,
    45	        source: PyRecordBatchReader,
    46	        batch_schema: PyArrowSchema,
    47	        predicate: String,
    48	        source_alias: Option<String>,
    49	        target_alias: Option<String>,
    50	        merge_schema: bool,
    51	        safe_cast: bool,
    52	        streamed_exec: bool,
    53	        max_spill_size: Option<usize>,
    54	        max_temp_directory_size: Option<u64>,
    55	        writer_properties: Option<PyWriterProperties>,
    56	        post_commithook_properties: Option<PyPostCommitHookProperties>,
    57	        commit_properties: Option<PyCommitProperties>,
    58	        custom_execute_handler: Option<Arc<dyn CustomExecuteHandler>>,
    59	    ) -> DeltaResult<Self> {
    60	        let ctx = create_session().into_inner();
    61	
    62	        let source = source
    63	            .into_reader()
    64	            .map_err(|e| DeltaTableError::generic(e.to_string()))?;
    65	
    66	        let source = maybe_lazy_cast_reader(source, batch_schema.into_inner());
    67	        let schema = source.schema();
    68	
    69	        let source_df = if streamed_exec {
    70	            let arrow_stream_batch_generator: Arc<RwLock<dyn LazyBatchGenerator>> =
    71	                Arc::new(RwLock::new(ArrowStreamBatchGenerator::new(source)));
    72	
    73	            let table_provider: Arc<dyn TableProvider> = Arc::new(LazyTableProvider::try_new(
    74	                schema.clone(),
    75	                vec![arrow_stream_batch_generator],
    76	            )?);
    77	            ctx.read_table(table_provider).unwrap()
    78	        } else {
    79	            let batches = vec![source.map(|batch| batch.unwrap()).collect::<Vec<_>>()];
    80	            let table_provider: Arc<dyn TableProvider> =
    81	                Arc::new(MemTable::try_new(schema.clone(), batches).unwrap());
    82	            ctx.read_table(table_provider).unwrap()
    83	        };
    84	
    85	        let mut cmd = MergeBuilder::new(log_store, Some(snapshot), predicate, source_df)
    86	            .with_safe_cast(safe_cast)
    87	            .with_streaming(streamed_exec);
    88	
    89	        if max_spill_size.is_some() || max_temp_directory_size.is_some() {
    90	            let session =
    91	                create_session_state_with_spill_config(max_spill_size, max_temp_directory_size);
    92	            cmd = cmd.with_session_state(Arc::new(session));
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        if let Some(src_alias) = &source_alias {
    96	            cmd = cmd.with_source_alias(src_alias);
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        if let Some(trgt_alias) = &target_alias {
   100	            cmd = cmd.with_target_alias(trgt_alias);
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        cmd = cmd.with_merge_schema(merge_schema);
   104	
   105	        if let Some(writer_props) = writer_properties {
   106	            cmd = cmd.with_writer_properties(set_writer_properties(writer_props)?);
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        if let Some(commit_properties) =
   110	            maybe_create_commit_properties(commit_properties, post_commithook_properties)
   111	        {
   112	            cmd = cmd.with_commit_properties(commit_properties);
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        if let Some(handler) = custom_execute_handler {
   116	            cmd = cmd.with_custom_execute_handler(handler);
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        Ok(Self {
   120	            _builder: Some(cmd),
   121	            source_alias,
   122	            target_alias,
   123	            merge_schema,
   124	            arrow_schema: schema,
   125	        })
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    pub fn execute(&mut self) -> DeltaResult<(DeltaTable, String)> {
   129	        let (table, metrics) = rt().block_on(self._builder.take().unwrap().into_future())?;
   130	        Ok((table, serde_json::to_string(&metrics).unwrap()))
   131	    }
   132	}

   134	#[pymethods]
   135	impl PyMergeBuilder {
   136	    #[getter]
   137	    fn get_arrow_schema(&self) -> PyArrowSchema {
   138	        PyArrowSchema::new(self.arrow_schema.clone())
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    #[pyo3(signature=(
   142	        updates,
   143	        predicate = None,
   144	    ))]
   145	    fn when_matched_update(
   146	        &mut self,
   147	        updates: HashMap<String, String>,
   148	        predicate: Option<String>,
   149	    ) -> PyResult<()> {
   150	        self._builder = match self._builder.take() {
   151	            Some(cmd) => Some(
   152	                cmd.when_matched_update(|mut update| {
   153	                    for (column, expression) in updates {
   154	                        update = update.update(column, expression)
   155	                    }
   156	                    if let Some(predicate) = predicate {
   157	                        update = update.predicate(predicate)
   158	                    };
   159	                    update
   160	                })
   161	                .map_err(PythonError::from)?,
   162	            ),
   163	            None => unreachable!(),
   164	        };
   165	        Ok(())
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    #[pyo3(signature=(
   169	        predicate = None,
   170	    ))]
   171	    fn when_matched_delete(&mut self, predicate: Option<String>) -> PyResult<()> {
   172	        self._builder = match self._builder.take() {
   173	            Some(cmd) => Some(
   174	                cmd.when_matched_delete(|mut delete| {
   175	                    if let Some(predicate) = predicate {
   176	                        delete = delete.predicate(predicate)
   177	                    };
   178	                    delete
   179	                })
   180	                .map_err(PythonError::from)?,

   200	                        insert = insert.set(column, expression)

   202	                    if let Some(predicate) = predicate {
   203	                        insert = insert.predicate(predicate)

   207	                .map_err(PythonError::from)?,

   209	            None => unreachable!(),
   210	        };
   211	        Ok(())
   212	    }

   242	        predicate = None,
   243	    ))]
   244	    fn when_not_matched_by_source_delete(&mut self, predicate: Option<String>) -> PyResult<()> {
   245	        self._builder = match self._builder.take() {
   246	            Some(cmd) => Some(
   247	                cmd.when_not_matched_by_source_delete(|mut delete| {
   248	                    if let Some(predicate) = predicate {
   249	                        delete = delete.predicate(predicate)
   250	                    };
   251	                    delete
   252	                })
   253	                .map_err(PythonError::from)?,
   254	            ),
   255	            None => unreachable!(),
   256	        };
   257	        Ok(())
   258	    }
   259	}
   260

  1765	    pub(crate) async fn setup_table(partitions: Option<Vec<&str>>) -> DeltaTable {
  1766	        let table_schema = get_delta_schema();
  1767	
  1768	        let table = DeltaTable::new_in_memory()

  1770	            .with_columns(table_schema.fields().cloned())
  1771	            .with_partition_columns(partitions.unwrap_or_default())
  1772	            .await
  1773	            .unwrap();
  1774	        assert_eq!(table.version(), Some(0));
  1775	        table
  1776	    }

  1779	    async fn test_merge_early_filter_does_not_row_filter_rewritten_files() {
  1780	        let schema = get_arrow_schema(&None);
  1781	        let table = setup_table(Some(vec!["modified"])).await;
  1782	        let table = write_data(table, &schema).await;
  1783	        assert_eq!(table.version(), Some(1));
  1784	        assert_eq!(table.snapshot().unwrap().log_data().num_files(), 2);
  1785	
  1786	        let ctx = SessionContext::new();
  1787	        let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(
  1788	            Arc::clone(&schema),
  1789	            vec![
  1790	                Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["A"])),
  1791	                Arc::new(arrow::array::Int32Array::from(vec![999])),
  1792	                Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["2021-02-01"])),
  1793	            ],
  1794	        )
  1795	        .unwrap();
  1796	        let source = ctx.read_batch(batch).unwrap();
  1797	
  1798	        let predicate = col("target.id")
  1799	            .eq(col("source.id"))
  1800	            .and(col("target.modified").eq(col("source.modified")));
  1801	
  1802	        let (table, metrics) = table
  1803	            .merge(source, predicate)
  1804	            .with_source_alias("source")
  1805	            .with_target_alias("target")
  1806	            .when_matched_update(|update| update.update("value", col("source.value")))
  1807	            .unwrap()
  1808	            .await
  1809	            .unwrap();
  1810	
  1811	        assert_eq!(metrics.num_target_files_scanned, 1);
  1812	        assert_eq!(metrics.num_target_files_skipped_during_scan, 1);
  1813	
  1814	        let expected = vec![
  1815	            "+----+-------+------------+",
  1816	            "| id | value | modified   |",
  1817	            "+----+-------+------------+",
  1818	            "| A  | 999   | 2021-02-01 |",
  1819	            "| B  | 10    | 2021-02-01 |",
  1820	            "| C  | 10    | 2021-02-02 |",
  1821	            "| D  | 100   | 2021-02-02 |",
  1822	            "+----+-------+------------+",
  1823	        ];
  1824	        let actual = get_data(&table).await;
  1825	        assert_batches_sorted_eq!(&expected, &actual);
  1826	    }

  1828	    #[tokio::test]
  1829	    async fn test_merge_metrics_derive_skipped_files_when_scan_skip_metric_missing() {
  1830	        let schema = get_arrow_schema(&None);
  1831	        let table = setup_table(Some(vec!["modified"])).await;
  1832	        let table = write_data(table, &schema).await;
  1833	        let pre_merge_files = table.snapshot().unwrap().log_data().num_files();
  1834	        assert_eq!(pre_merge_files, 2);
  1835	
  1836	        let ctx = SessionContext::new();
  1837	        let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(
  1838	            Arc::clone(&schema),
  1839	            vec![
  1840	                Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["A"])),
  1841	                Arc::new(arrow::array::Int32Array::from(vec![999])),
  1842	                Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["2021-02-01"])),
  1843	            ],
  1844	        )
  1845	        .unwrap();
  1846	        let source = ctx.read_batch(batch).unwrap();
  1847	        let predicate = col("target.id")
  1848	            .eq(col("source.id"))
  1849	            .and(col("target.modified").eq(col("source.modified")));
  1850	
  1851	        let (_table, metrics) = table
  1852	            .merge(source, predicate)
  1853	            .with_source_alias("source")
  1854	            .with_target_alias("target")
  1855	            .when_matched_update(|update| update.update("value", col("source.value")))
  1856	            .unwrap()
  1857	            .await
  1858	            .unwrap();
  1859	
  1860	        assert_eq!(metrics.num_target_files_scanned, 1);
  1861	        assert_eq!(
  1862	            metrics.num_target_files_skipped_during_scan,
  1863	            pre_merge_files.saturating_sub(metrics.num_target_files_scanned)
  1864	        );
  1865	        assert_eq!(metrics.num_target_files_skipped_during_scan, 1);
  1866	    }

  1881	        );

  1883	            predicates[1],
  1884	            col(Column::new_unqualified("modified")).eq(lit("2021-02-01"))
  1885	        );
  1886	    }

Now let me understand the issue better by looking at the merge execution flow. The key insight is:

1. A full outer join is performed between source and target
2. If multiple source rows match the same target row, the join produces multiple rows with both `SOURCE_COLUMN` = true and `TARGET_COLUMN` = true
3. Currently, all these matched rows go through the `when_matched_update` logic and end up being written out, effectively duplicating the target row

The fix should detect this situation and raise an error. Let me look at how this can be detected. The best place seems to be in the merge execution, where we could check if there are any target rows that appear multiple times in the matched set.

Let me look at the full merge flow more carefully - specifically the part where the merge barrier processes batches:

Now I have a good understanding. The issue is that when multiple source rows match the same target row, the join produces multiple output rows for that target row. The MERGE operation should validate that there is at most one source row per target row for the matched case.

Let me look at how the Databricks/Spark implementation handles this. The standard SQL MERGE semantics say:

> "If there is more than one match of a single target row in the source table, an error is raised."

This applies to `WHEN MATCHED` clauses. Let me now implement the fix.

The approach should be:
1. After the join, check if there are duplicate target rows in the matched set (where both SOURCE_COLUMN and TARGET_COLUMN are true)
2. If duplicates are found and there are match operations (update/delete), raise an error

Let me look at where the join happens and where we could add this validation:

The join is at line 951. After the join, we could check for duplicate matches. But the join result is a DataFrame, and checking for duplicates would require another aggregation. Alternatively, we could check after the merge is executed by counting outputs vs inputs.

Actually, looking at this more carefully, the proper fix should be to check that for `when_matched_update` and `when_matched_delete`, there should be at most one source row per target row. The check should happen before we start writing data.

Let me look at how other Delta connectors (like the Scala/Java one) handle this:

Looking at the Spark implementation, they add a check that counts the number of source rows matching each target row and raises an error if the count > 1. This is typically done by adding a window function or group-by on the join result.

Let me implement this check. The approach:
1. After the join, if there are match operations (update or delete), validate that no target row appears more than once in the matched set
2. To do this, we can group by target columns and count, filtering where count > 1

But actually, we need to be careful about when to raise this error. The error should only be raised when:
- There are `when_matched_update` or `when_matched_delete` clauses
- Multiple source rows match the same target row

> "If the number of rows in <source table reference> that satisfy the search condition for a target row is greater than 1, then it is an exception."

/// Validates that no target row is matched by more than one source row.
/// This is required by the SQL standard for MERGE operations that include
/// WHEN MATCHED clauses (update or delete).
///
/// We detect duplicates by:
/// 1. Filtering to only matched rows (both SOURCE_COLUMN and TARGET_COLUMN are true)
/// 2. Grouping by all target columns and counting rows
/// 3. If any group has count > 1, raising an error
async fn validate_no_duplicate_matches(
    join: &DataFrame,
    state: &SessionState,
    source_name: &TableReference<'"'"'_>,
    target_name: &TableReference<'"'"'_>,
    source_alias: &Option<String>,
    target_alias: &Option<String>,
) -> DeltaResult<()> {
    let matched = col(SOURCE_COLUMN)
        .is_true()
        .and(col(TARGET_COLUMN).is_true());

    // Get the target columns: those that belong to the target table
    let join_schema = join.schema().clone();
    let target_cols: Vec<Expr> = join_schema
        .columns()
        .iter()
        .filter(|col| {
            // Check if the column belongs to the target table
            match &col.relation {
                Some(relation) => {
                    let target_name_str = match target_alias {
                        Some(alias) => alias.as_str(),
                        None => UNNAMED_TABLE,
                    };
                    relation.table() == target_name_str
                }
                None => {
                    // Unqualified columns: check if they exist in target schema
                    // but not in source schema (e.g., internal columns like __delta_rs_target)
                    false
                }
            }
        })
        .map(|col| col.clone())
        .collect();

    if target_cols.is_empty() {
        // Should not happen, but if we can'"'"'t determine target columns, skip validation
        return Ok(());
    }

    // Build aggregation: group by all target columns, count rows
    let count_expr = Expr::count(lit(1)).alias("__delta_rs_dup_count");
    let filtered = join.clone().filter(matched)?;
    let grouped = filtered.aggregate(target_cols.clone(), vec![count_expr])?;
    let duplicates = grouped.filter(col("__delta_rs_dup_count").gt(lit(1 as i64)))?;

    // Collect the result to check if there are any duplicates
    let batches = duplicates.collect().await.map_err(|e| {
        DeltaTableError::Generic(format!("Failed to check for duplicate matches: {e}"))
    })?;

    if !batches.is_empty() && batches.iter().any(|b| b.num_rows() > 0) {
        return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic(
            "Multiple source rows matched the same target row. This is not permitted for MERGE operations with WHEN MATCHED clauses. Please ensure that the source table contains at most one matching row per target row.".to_string(),
        ));
    }

    Ok(())
}

  1651	/// Validates that no target row is matched by more than one source row.
  1652	/// This is required by the SQL standard for MERGE operations that include
  1653	/// WHEN MATCHED clauses (update or delete).
  1654	///
  1655	/// We detect duplicates by:
  1656	/// 1. Filtering to only matched rows (both SOURCE_COLUMN and TARGET_COLUMN are true)
  1657	/// 2. Grouping by all target columns and counting rows
  1658	/// 3. If any group has count > 1, raising an error
